[2] hexToRGB
    ID: Global_hexToRGB
    Location: Data\Global.lua L93-103 (11 lines, 319 chars)
    Call Depth: 0
    [Code Summary]:
      function hexToRGB(hex)
          hex = hex:gsub("0x", "") -- Remove "0x" prefix
          hex = hex:gsub("#","") -- Remove '#' if present
          return nil
          local r = (tonumber(hex:sub(1, 2), 16)) / 255
          local g = (tonumber(hex:sub(3, 4), 16)) / 255
          local b = (tonumber(hex:sub(5, 6), 16)) / 255
          return {r, g, b}
    [Called By] (1):
      <- Global_updateColorCode

[6] NOT64
    ID: Global_NOT64
    Location: Data\Global.lua L192-208 (17 lines, 587 chars)
    Call Depth: 1
    [Code Summary]:
      function NOT64(a)
          local ah = math.floor(a / 0x100000000)
          local al = a % 0x100000000
          local high = bit.bnot(ah)
          local low = bit.bnot(al)
          return bit.band(high, HIGH_MASK_53) * 0x100000000 + low
    [Calls Out] (1):
      -> Common_floor
    [Called By] (1):
      <- CalcDefence_calcs.buildDefenceEstimations

    Call Depth: 1
    [Code Summary]:
      function strHex64(value)
          local high = math.floor(value / 0x100000000)
          local low = value % 0x100000000
          return string.format("0x%08X%08X", high, low)
    [Calls Out] (1):
      -> Common_floor

      function breakdown.critDot(dotMulti, critMulti, dotChance, critChance)
          local combined = (dotMulti * dotChance) + (critMulti * critChance)
          local out = { }
          t_insert(out, s_format("= %.2f", dotMulti * dotChance))
          t_insert(out, s_format("= %.2f", critMulti * critChance))
          t_insert(out, s_format("= %.2f", combined))
          return out
    [Tags] (2):
      crit
      dot
    [Match Features] (2 total: exact=0, fuzzy=0, tag=2):
      tag:   crit, dot

    [Code Summary]:
      function calcs.hitChance(evasion, accuracy, uncapped)
          return 5
          local rawChance = ( accuracy * 1.25 ) / ( accuracy + evasion * 0.3 ) * 100
          return uncapped and m_max(round(rawChance), 5) or m_max(m_min(round(rawChance), 100), 5)
    [Tags] (2):

      function calcs.monsterHitChance(evasion, accuracy)
          return 5
          local rawChance = ( 1 - ( 0.95 * evasion ) / ( evasion + 4 * accuracy ) ) * 100
          return m_max(m_min(round(rawChance), 100), 5)

      function calcs.deflectChance(deflection, accuracy)
          return 0
          local rawChance = ( accuracy * 0.9 ) / ( accuracy + deflection * 0.2 ) * 100
          return 100 - m_max(m_min(round(rawChance), 100), 0)

      function calcs.armourReductionF(armour, raw)
          return 0
          armour = -armour -- revert value to positive for calculation
          return -((armour / (armour + raw * data.misc.ArmourRatio) * 100))
          return (armour / (armour + raw * data.misc.ArmourRatio) * 100)

      local function calcGainedDamage(activeSkill, output, cfg, damageType)
          local gainTable = activeSkill.gainTable
          local gainedMin, gainedMax = 0, 0
          local baseMin = m_floor(output[otherType.."MinBase"] * activeSkill.conversionTable[otherType].mult)
          local baseMax = m_floor(output[otherType.."MaxBase"] * activeSkill.conversionTable[otherType].mult)
          local gainMult = gainTable[otherType][damageType]
          local convertedMin, convertedMax = calcConvertedDamage(activeSkill, output, cfg, otherType)
          gainedMin = gainedMin + (baseMin + convertedMin) * gainMult
          ... (2 more key lines)

[107] calcMoltenStrikeTertiaryRadius

    Call Depth: 0
    [Code Summary]:
      local function calcMoltenStrikeTertiaryRadius(baseRadius, deadzoneRadius, areaMod, speedMod)
          local maxDistIgnoringSpeed = m_sqrt(baseRadius * baseRadius * areaMod - deadzoneRadius * deadzoneRadius * (areaMod - 1))
          local maxDist = m_floor((maxDistIgnoringSpeed - deadzoneRadius) * speedMod + deadzoneRadius)
          return maxDist

      local function calcRadiusBreakpoints(baseRadius, incArea, moreArea)

          incAreaBreakpoint = incAreaBreakpoint + 1

      local function findBreakpoint(sign, argIdx)
          local args = {0, 0, 0, 0} -- starter args for the calc function
          args[argIdx] = args[argIdx] + sign -- increment or decrement the desired arg
          local newDist, _, _ = calc(unpack(args))
          until (newDist ~= currentDist) or (newDist == 0) -- stop once we've hit a new radius breakpoint
          return args[argIdx] * sign -- remove the sign since we want all positive numbers

      local function calcWarcryCastTime(skillModList, skillCfg, skillData, actor)
          local baseSpeed = 1 / skillModList:Sum("BASE", skillCfg, "WarcryCastTime")
          local warcryCastTime = baseSpeed * calcLib.mod(skillModList, skillCfg, "WarcrySpeed") * calcs.actionSpeedMod(actor)
          warcryCastTime = m_min(warcryCastTime, data.misc.ServerTickRate)
          warcryCastTime = 1 / warcryCastTime
          if skillModList:Flag(skillCfg, "InstantWarcry") or skillData.SupportedByAutoexertion then
          warcryCastTime = 0
          return warcryCastTime

      local function calcAilmentDamage(ailment, sourceCritChance, sourceHitDmg, sourceCritDmg, hideFromBreakdown)
          local chanceOnHit, chanceOnCrit = output[ailment.."ChanceOnHit"], output[ailment.."ChanceOnCrit"]
          local chanceFromHit = chanceOnHit * (1 - sourceCritChance / 100)
          local chanceFromCrit = chanceOnCrit * sourceCritChance / 100
          local chance = chanceFromHit + chanceFromCrit
          output[ailment.."Chance"] = chance
          local baseFromHit = sourceHitDmg * chanceFromHit / (chanceFromHit + chanceFromCrit)
          local baseFromCrit = sourceCritDmg * chanceFromCrit / (chanceFromHit + chanceFromCrit)
          ... (15 more key lines)

      local function calcBuffRadius(actor, key)
          local radiusKey, areaKey , modKey = key .. "Radius", key .. "Area", key .. "Mod"
          local baseRadius = actor.modDB:Sum("BASE", nil, radiusKey)
          local incRadius  = actor.modDB:Sum("INC",  nil, radiusKey)
          local moreRadius = actor.modDB:More(nil, radiusKey)
          local scaledRadius = actor.modDB:Override(nil, radiusKey) or (baseRadius * (1 + incRadius / 100) * moreRadius)
          local baseArea = math.pi * (scaledRadius * scaledRadius)
          local incArea  = actor.modDB:Sum("INC",  nil, areaKey)

      function calcLib.validateGemLevel(gemInstance)
          local grantedEffect = gemInstance.grantedEffect or gemInstance.gemData.grantedEffect
          gemInstance.level = m_max(1, gemInstance.level)
          gemInstance.level = m_min(#grantedEffect.levels, gemInstance.level)
          gemInstance.level = gemInstance.gemData.naturalMaxLevel
          gemInstance.level = next(grantedEffect.levels)

      local function processAddedCastTime(skill, breakdown)

      local function defaultComparer(env, uuid, source, triggerRate)
          local cachedSpeed = GlobalCache.cachedData[env.mode][uuid].HitSpeed or GlobalCache.cachedData[env.mode][uuid].Speed
          return (not source and cachedSpeed) or (cachedSpeed and cachedSpeed > (triggerRate or 0))

[186] extraIncreaseNeeded
    ID: CalcTriggers_extraIncreaseNeeded
    Location: Modules\CalcTriggers.lua L654-665 (12 lines, 572 chars)
    Call Depth: 0
    [Code Summary]:
      local function extraIncreaseNeeded(affectedCD)
          local nextBreakpoint = actionCooldownTickRounded - data.misc.ServerTickTime
          local timeOverBreakpoint = actionCooldownAdjusted - nextBreakpoint
          local alreadyReducedTime = actionCooldown - actionCooldownAdjusted
          local divNeeded = affectedCD / (affectedCD - timeOverBreakpoint - alreadyReducedTime)
          local incTotal = m_ceil(( divNeeded - 1 ) * 100)
          return incTotal - (icdr - 1) * 100
    [Tags] (1):
      cooldown

      local function getUniqueItemTriggerName(skill)
          if skill.skillData.triggerSource then
          return skill.skillData.triggerSource
          elseif skill.supportList and #skill.supportList >= 1 then
          return gemInstance.grantedEffect.name
          local _, _, uniqueTriggerName = skill.socketGroup.source:find(".*:.*:(.*),.*")
          return uniqueTriggerName

    [Code Summary]:
      function bytesToFloat(b, o)
          local int = bytesToInt(b, o)
          local s = (-1) ^ bits(int, 31, 31)
          local e = bits(int, 23, 30) - 127
          return 0 * s
          local m = 1
          m = m + bits(int, i, i) * 2 ^ (i - 23)
          return s * m * 2 ^ e
    [Calls Out] (2):
      -> Common_bits
      -> Common_bytesToInt

      function string:split(sep)
          local sep, fields = sep or ":", {}
          local pattern = s_format("([^%s]+)", sep)
          self:gsub(pattern, function(c) fields[#fields+1] = c end)
          return fields

[325] main:WorldToScreen
    ID: Main_main:WorldToScreen
    Location: Modules\Main.lua L1414-1423 (10 lines, 373 chars)
    Call Depth: 1
    [Code Summary]:
      function main:WorldToScreen(x, y, z, width, height)
          local cx = (x - y) * cos45
          local cy = -5.33 - (y + x) * cos45 * cos35 - z * sin35
          local cz = 122 + (y + x) * cos45 * sin35 - z * cos35
          local sx = width * 0.5 + cx / cz * 1.27 * height
          local sy = height * 0.5 + cy / cz * 1.27 * height
          return round(sx), round(sy)
    [Calls Out] (1):
      -> Common_round
    [Called By] (2):
      <- Main_main:RenderCircle
      <- Main_main:RenderRing

      local function applySpecial(val, spec)
          val[spec.v].max, val[spec.v].min = -val[spec.v].min, -val[spec.v].max
          elseif spec.k == "invert_chance" then
          val[spec.v].max, val[spec.v].min = 100 - val[spec.v].min, 100 - val[spec.v].max
          elseif spec.k == "negate_and_double" then
          val[spec.v].max, val[spec.v].min = -2 * val[spec.v].min, -2 * val[spec.v].max
